This means these endpoints are not protected by Loki itself by default.\n\n**The /ready Endpoint:**\nThe /ready endpoint can be accessed without authentication, while the root endpoint is protected by basic authentication. This is typically intentional for health checks, but demonstrates the granular nature of endpoint protection in Loki.\n\n**Recommendation:**\nThe search results indicate this is a known security concern in Loki deployments, suggesting that these diagnostic and metrics endpoints should be protected through a reverse proxy or similar mechanism if they need to be restricted from public access.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":"toolu_01DKsjydULJCB6oAzyb9p3iC","session_id":"83d097a7-7669-4bc3-918f-face5aa2a6d6","uuid":"b844051b-ffad-4a4f-aea4-8868a2cb14ab"}

If this field is set _before_ the API module is\n    69→\t// initialized, the custom config handler will be used instead of\n    70→\t// DefaultConfigHandler.\n    71→\tCustomConfigHandler ConfigHandler `yaml:\"-\"`\n    72→}\n    73→\n    74→// RegisterFlags adds the flags required to config this to the given FlagSet.\n    75→func (cfg *Config) RegisterFlags(f *flag.FlagSet) {\n    76→\tf.BoolVar(&cfg.SkipLabelNameValidationHeader, \"api.skip-label-name-validation-header-enabled\", false, \"Allows to skip label name validation via X-Mimir-SkipLabelNameValidation header on the http write path. Use with caution as it breaks PromQL. Allowing this for external clients allows any client to send invalid label names. After enabling it, requests with a specific HTTP header set to true will not have label names validated.\")\n    77→\tf.BoolVar(&cfg.SkipLabelCountValidationHeader, \"api.skip-label-count-validation-header-enabled\", false, \"Allows to disable enforcement of the label count limit \\\"max_label_names_per_series\\\" via X-Mimir-SkipLabelCountValidation header on the http write path. Allowing this for external clients allows any client to send invalid label counts. After enabling it, requests with a specific HTTP header set to true will not have label counts validated.\")\n    78→\tcfg.RegisterFlagsWithPrefix(\"\", f)\n    79→}\n    80→\n    81→// RegisterFlagsWithPrefix adds the flags required to config this to the given FlagSet with the set prefix.\n    82→func (cfg *Config) RegisterFlagsWithPrefix(prefix string, f *flag.FlagSet) {\n    83→\tf.StringVar(&cfg.AlertmanagerHTTPPrefix, prefix+\"http.alertmanager-http-prefix\", \"/alertmanager\", \"HTTP URL path under which the Alertmanager ui and api will be served.\")\n    84→\tf.StringVar(&cfg.PrometheusHTTPPrefix, prefix+\"http.prometheus-http-prefix\", \"/prometheus\", \"HTTP URL path under which the Prometheus api will be served.\")\n    85→}\n    86→\n    87→type API struct {\n    88→\tAuthMiddleware middleware.Interface\n    89→\n    90→\tcfg       Config\n    91→\tserver    *server.Server\n    92→\tlogger    log.Logger\n    93→\tsourceIPs *middleware.SourceIPExtractor\n    94→\tindexPage *IndexPageContent\n    95→}\n    96→\n    97→func New(cfg Config, federationCfg tenantfederation.Config, serverCfg server.Config, s *server.Server, logger log.Logger) (*API, error) {\n    98→\t// Ensure the encoded path is used. Required for the rules API\n    99→\ts.HTTP.UseEncodedPath()\n   100→\n   101→\tvar sourceIPs *middleware.SourceIPExtractor\n   102→\tif serverCfg.LogSourceIPs {\n   103→\t\tvar err error\n   104→\t\tsourceIPs, err = middleware.NewSourceIPs(serverCfg.LogSourceIPsHeader, serverCfg.LogSourceIPsRegex, serverCfg.LogSourceIPsFull)\n   105→\t\tif err != nil {\n   106→\t\t\t// This should have already been caught in the Server creation\n   107→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   108→\t\t}\n   109→\t}\n   110→\n   111→\tapi := &API{\n   112→\t\tcfg:            cfg,\n   113→\t\tAuthMiddleware: cfg.HTTPAuthMiddleware,\n   114→\t\tserver:         s,\n   115→\t\tlogger:         logger,\n   116→\t\tsourceIPs:      sourceIPs,\n   117→\t\tindexPage:      newIndexPageContent(serverCfg.PathPrefix),\n   118→\t}\n   119→\n   120→\t// If no authentication middleware is present in the config, use the default authentication middleware.\n   121→\tif api.AuthMiddleware == nil {\n   122→\t\tapi.AuthMiddleware = middleware.AuthenticateUser\n   123→\t}\n   124→\n   125→\t// Unconditionally add middleware that ensures we only accept requests with an expected number of tenants\n   126→\t// that is applied after any existing auth middleware has run. Only a single tenant is allowed when federation\n   127→\t// is disabled. If federation is enabled, there is optionally a max number of tenants that is supported.\n   128→\tapi.AuthMiddleware = middleware.Merge(api.AuthMiddleware, newTenantValidationMiddleware(federationCfg.Enabled, federationCfg.MaxTenants))\n   129→\n   130→\treturn api, nil\n   131→}\n   132→\n   133→// RegisterDeprecatedRoute behaves in a similar way to RegisterRoute. RegisterDeprecatedRoute also logs warnings on\n   134→// invocations of the deprecated endpoints.\n   135→func (a *API) RegisterDeprecatedRoute(path string, handler http.Handler, auth, gzipEnabled bool, method string, methods ...string) {\n   136→\tmethods = append([]string{method}, methods...)\n   137→\thandler = a.deprecatedHandler(handler)\n   138→\tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"api: registering deprecated route\", \"methods\", strings.Join(methods, \",\"), \"path\", path, \"auth\", auth, \"gzip\", gzipEnabled)\n   139→\ta.newRoute(path, handler, false, auth, gzipEnabled, methods...)\n   140→}\n   141→\n   142→func (a *API) deprecatedHandler(next http.Handler) http.Handler {\n   143→\tl := util_log.NewRateLimitedLogger(time.Minute, a.logger, time.Now)\n   144→\n   145→\treturn http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   146→\t\tlevel.Warn(l).Log(\"msg\", \"api: received a request on a deprecated endpoint\", \"path\", r.URL.Path, \"method\", r.Method)\n   147→\t\tnext.ServeHTTP(w, r)\n   148→\t})\n   149→}\n   150→\n   151→// RegisterRoute registers a single route enforcing HTTP methods. A single\n   152→// route is expected to be specific about which HTTP methods are supported.\n   153→func (a *API) RegisterRoute(path string, handler http.Handler, auth, gzipEnabled bool, method string, methods ...string) {\n   154→\tmethods = append([]string{method}, methods...)\n   155→\tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"api: registering route\", \"methods\", strings.Join(methods, \",\"), \"path\", path, \"auth\", auth, \"gzip\", gzipEnabled)\n   156→\ta.newRoute(path, handler, false, auth, gzipEnabled, methods...)\n   157→}\n   158→\n   159→func (a *API) RegisterRoutesWithPrefix(prefix string, handler http.Handler, auth, gzipEnabled bool, methods ...string) {\n   160→\tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"api: registering route\", \"methods\", strings.Join(methods, \",\"), \"prefix\", prefix, \"auth\", auth, \"gzip\", gzipEnabled)\n   161→\ta.newRoute(prefix, handler, true, auth, gzipEnabled, methods...)\n   162→}\n   163→\n   164→func (a *API) newRoute(path string, handler http.Handler, isPrefix, auth, gzip bool, methods ...string) (route *mux.Route) {\n   165→\t// Propagate the consistency level on all HTTP routes.\n   166→\t// They are not used everywhere, but for consistency and less surprise it's added everywhere.\n   167→\thandler = propagation.Middleware(&querierapi.ConsistencyExtractor{}).Wrap(handler)\n   168→\n   169→\tif auth {\n   170→\t\thandler = a.AuthMiddleware.Wrap(handler)\n   171→\t}\n   172→\tif gzip {\n   173→\t\thandler = gziphandler.GzipHandler(handler)\n   174→\t}\n   175→\tif isPrefix {\n   176→\t\troute = a.server.HTTP.PathPrefix(path)\n   177→\t} else {\n   178→\t\troute = a.server.HTTP.Path(path)\n   179→\t}\n   180→\tif len(methods) > 0 {\n   181→\t\troute = route.Methods(methods...)\n   182→\t}\n   183→\troute = route.Handler(handler)\n   184→\n   185→\treturn route\n   186→}\n   187→\n   188→// RegisterAlertmanager registers endpoints that are associated with the alertmanager.\n   189→func (a
